ManusmR^iti
Typed, analyshed and proofread by M.YANO and Y.IKAR^iI 
(May-June 1991, January-April1992, March-April 1996)

 
K: ManusmR^iti with the Shanskrit Commentary Manvartha-MuktAvalI of KullUka 
BhaTTa, ed. J.L.Shhastri 1983.  (Compared with the edition of 
Kashi Shkt Sheries 114 ed. Haragovinda Shastri.)
M: ManusmR^iti with the commentary of MedAtithi, 2vols. Calcutta 1967
M: Manu-smR^iti with the "ManubhAShya" of MedhAtithi, ed. GaGgAnAtha JhA, 
GOI 1932,1939 rep. 1992	
 
Text is based upon K, and M's variant is given at each pada-end.
There are verses which are found only in K or M. The difference of
the shloka-numbering of chapter between K and M is noticed. 
 
Shome sandhis have been dissolved and word division marks such as
"-" and "." are introduced in the text in order to have easy 
identification of individual word form.
"-" indicates resolve of the external sandhi.
"." indicates word division within a compound.

[M:] variants of MedhAtithi's 
Different numbering of verses between M and K is noted.

<B 1>

M1.01a/ manum ekAgram AsInam abhigamya) maharShayaH |
M1.01c/ pratipUjya) yathAnyAyam idaM vacanam abruvan) ||
M1.02a/ bhagavan sarvavarNAnAM yathAvad anupUrvashaH |
M1.02c/ antaraprabhavAnAM ca dharmAn no vaktum arhasi) ||
M1.03a/ tvam eko hy asya sarvasya vidhAnasya svayaMbhuvaH |
M1.03c/ acintyasya-aprameyasya kAryatattvArthavit prabho ||
M1.04a/ sa taiH pR^iShTas) tathA samyag amita.ojA mahAtmabhiH |
M1.04c/ pratyuvAca)-arcya) tAn sarvAn maharShIn- shrUyatAm) iti ||
M1.05a/ AsId) idam tamobhUtam a.prajJAtam a.lakShaNam |
M1.05c/ a.pratarkyam a.vijJeyaM prasuptam iva sarvataH ||
M1.06a/ tataH svayaMbhUr bhagavAn avyakto vyaJjayann) idam |
M1.06c/ mahAbhUtAdi vR^itta.ojAH prAdur AsIt) tamonudaH ||
M1.07a/ yo 'asAv atIndriyagrAhyaH sUkShmo 'avyaktaH sanAtanaH |
M1.07c/ sarvabhUtamayo 'acintyaH sa eva svayam udbabhau) ||| [M. sa eSha]
M1.08a/ so 'abhidhyAya) sharIrAt svAt sisR^ikShur vividhAH prajAH |
M1.08c/ apa eva sasarja)-Adau tAsu vIryam avAsR^ijat) ||
M1.09a/ tad aNDam abhavadd) haimaM sahasrAMshusama.prabham | 
M1.09c/ tasmiJ jajJe) svayaM brahmA sarvalokapitAmahaH ||
M1.10a/ Apo narA iti proktA) Apo vai narasUnavaH |
M1.10c/ tA yad asyAyanaM pUrvaM tena nArAyaNaH smR^itaH ||
M1.11a/ yat tat kAraNam avyaktaM nityaM sad.asad.AtmakaM |
M1.11c/ tad.visR^iShTaH sa puruSho loke brahmA-iti kIrtyate) ||

M1.12a/ tasminn aNDe sa bhagavAn uShitvA) parivatsaram |
M1.12c/ svayam evAtmano dhyAnAt tad aNDam akarod) dvidhA ||
M1.13a/ tAbhyAM sa shakalAbhyAM ca divaM bhUmiM ca nirmame) |
M1.13c/ madhye vyoma dishash ca-aShTAv apAM sthAnaM ca shAshvataM ||
M1.14a/ udbabarha)-Atmanash ca-eva manaH sad.asad.Atmakam |
M1.14c/ manasash ca-apy ahaMkAram abhimantAram Ishvaram || [M. ahaGkAram]

M1.15c/ viShayANAM grahItR^iR^iNi shanaiH paJca.indriyANi ca ||
M1.16a/ teShAM tv avayavAn sUkShmAn ShaNNAm apy amita.ojasAm |
M1.16c/ saMniveshya)-AtmamAtrAsu sarvabhUtAni nirmame) || [M. sanniveshya]
M1.17a/ yan mUrti.avayavAH sUkShmAs tAni-imAny Ashrayanti) ShaT |
M1.17c/ tasmAt-sharIram ity Ahus) tasya mUrtiM manIShiNaH ||
M1.18a/ tad Avishanti) bhUtAni mahAnti saha karmabhiH |
M1.18c/ manash ca-avayavaiH sUkShmaiH sarvabhUtakR^id avyayam ||
M1.19a/ teShAm idaM tu saptAnAM puruShANAM mahA.ojasAm |
M1.19c/ sUkShmAbhyo mUrtimAtrAbhyaH saMbhavaty) avyayAd vyayam ||
M1.20a/ AdyAdyasya guNaM tv eShAm avApnoti) paraH paraH |
M1.20c/ yo yo yAvatithash ca-eShAM sa sa tAvad guNaH smR^itaH ||
M1.21a/ sarveShAM tu sa nAmAni karmANi ca pR^ithak pR^ithak |
M1.21c/ vedashabdebhya eva-Adau pR^ithak saMsthAsh ca nirmame) ||
M1.22a/ karmAtmanAM ca devAnAM so 'asR^ijat) prANinAM prabhuH |
M1.22c/ sAdhyAnAM ca gaNaM sUkShmaM yajJaM ca-eva sanAtanam ||
M1.23a/ agni.vAyu.ravibhyas tu trayaM brahma sanAtanam |
M1.23c/ dudoha) yajJasiddhi.artham R^ic.yajus.sAma.lakShaNam ||

M1.24c/ saritaH sAgarAn-shailAn samAni viShamAni ca ||

M1.26a/ karmaNAM ca vivekArthaM dharma.adharmau vyavecayat) | [K:vivekAya ]
M1.26c/ dvandvair ayojayac) ca-imAH sukha.duHkhAdibhiH prajAH ||

M1.33c/ taM mAM vitta)-asya sarvasya sraShTAraM dvijasattamAH ||

M1.40a/ kR^imi.kITa.pataGgAMsh ca yUkA.makShika.matkuNam |
M1.40c/ sarvaM ca daMsha.mashakaM sthAvaraM ca pR^ithagvidham ||
M1.41a/ evam etair idaM sarvaM mad.niyogAn mahAtmabhiH |
M1.41c/ yathAkarma tapoyogAt sR^iShTaM) sthAvara.jaGgamam ||
M1.42a/ yeShAM tu yAdR^iShaM karma bhUtAnAm iha kIrtitam) |
M1.42c/ tat tathA vo 'abhidhAsyAmi) kramayogaM ca janmani ||

M1.43c/ rakShAMsi ca pishAcAsh ca manuShyAsh ca jarAyujAH || [M.manuShAsh ca ]

M1.45a/ svedajaM daMsha.mashakaM yUkA.makShika.matkuNam |

<B 5> 

M5.01a/ shrutvA-etAn R^iShayo dharmAn snAtakasya yathA.uditAn |
M5.01c/ idam Ucur mahAtmAnam anala.prabhavaM bhR^igum ||

M5.03c/ shrUyatAM yena doSheNa mR^ityur viprAn jighAMsati ||
M5.04a/ anabhyAsena vedAnAm AcArasya ca varjanAt |

M5.05c/ abhakShyANi dvijAtInAm amedhya.prabhavAni ca ||
M5.06a/ lohitAn vR^ikShaniryAsAn vR^ishcana.prabhavAMs tathA | [M.vrashcana.prabhavAMs ]

M6.66a/ dUShito 'api cared dharmaM yatra tatra-Ashrame rataH | [M.bhUShito 'api ]

M6.67a/ phalaM katakavR^ikShasya yady apy ambuprasAdakam |
M6.67c/ na nAmagrahaNAd eva tasya vAri prasIdati ||
M6.68a/ saMrakShaNArthaM jantUnAM rAtrAv ahani vA sadA |
M6.68c/ sharIrasya-atyaye ca-eva samIkShya vasudhAM caret ||
M6.69a/ ahnA rAtryA ca yAJ jantUn hinasty ajJAnato yatiH | 
M6.69c/ teShAM snAtvA vishuddhyarthaM prANAyAmAn ShaD Acaret ||
M6.70a/ prANAyAmA brAhmaNasya trayo 'api vidhivat kR^itAH |
M6.70c/ vyAhR^iti.praNavair yuktA vijJeyaM paramaM tapaH ||
M6.71a/ dahyante dhmAyamAnAnAM dhAtUnAM hi yathA malAH |
M6.71c/ tathA-indriyANAM dahyante doShAH prANasya nigrahAt ||
M6.72a/ prANAyamair dahed doShAn dhAraNAbhish ca kilbiSham |
M6.72c/ pratyAhAreNa saMsargAn dhyAnena-an.IshvarAn guNAn ||
M6.73a/ uccAvaceShu bhUteShu durjJeyAm akR^ita.AtmabhiH |
M6.73c/ dhyAnayogena saMpashyed gatim asya-antarAtmanaH ||
M6.74a/ samyagdarshanasaMpannaH karmabhir na nibadhyate |
M6.74c/ darshanena vihInas tu saMsAraM pratipadyate ||
M6.75a/ ahiMsayA-indriya.a.saGgair vaidikaish ca-eva karmabhiH |
M6.75c/ tapasash caraNaish ca-ugraiH sAdhayanti-iha tatpadam ||
M6.76a/ asthi.sthUNaM snAyuyutaM mAMsa.shoNita.lepanam |
M6.76c/ carmAvanaddhaM dur.gandhi pUrNaM mUtra.purIShayoH |
M6.77a/ jarA.shokasamAviShTaM rogAyatanam Aturam |
M6.77c/ rajasvalam anityaM ca bhUtAvAsam imaM tyajet ||
M6.78a/ nadIkUlaM yathA vR^ikSho vR^ikShaM vA shakunir yathA |
M6.78c/ tathA tyajann imaM dehaM kR^icchrAd grAhAd vimucyate ||
M6.79a/ priyeShu sveShu sukR^itam apriyeShu ca duShkR^itam |
M6.79c/ visR^ijya dhyAnayogena brahma-abhyeti sanAtanam ||
M6.80a/ yadA bhAvena bhavati sarvabhAveShu niHspR^ihaH |
M6.80c/ tadA sukham avApnoti pretya ca-iha ca shAshvatam ||
M6.81a/ anena vidhinA sarvAMs tyaktvA saGgAn-shanaiH shanaiH |
M6.81c/ sarvadvandvavinirmukto brahmaNy eva-avatiShThate ||
M6.82a/ dhyAnikaM sarvam eva-etad yad etad abhishabditam |
M6.82c/ na hy an.adhyAtmavit kash cit kriyAphalam upAshnute ||
M6.83a/ adhiyajJaM brahma japed Adhidaivikam eva ca |
M6.83c/ AdhyAtmikaM ca satataM vedAntAbhihitaM ca yat ||
M6.84a/ idaM sharaNam ajJAnAm idam eva vijAnatAm |
M6.84c/ idam anvicchatAM svargam idam Anantyam icchatAm ||
M6.85a/ anena kramayogena parivrajati yo dvijaH |
M6.85c/ sa vidhUya-iha pApmAnaM paraM brahma-adhigacchati ||

M6.86a/ eSha dharmo 'anushiShTo vo yatInAM niyata.AtmanAm |
M6.86c/ vedasaMnyAsikAnAM tu karmayogaM nibodhata ||
M6.87a/ brahmacArI gR^ihasthash ca vAnaprastho yatis tathA |
M6.87c/ ete gR^ihastha.prabhavAsh catvAraH pR^ithag AshramAH ||
M6.88a/ sarve 'api kramashas tv ete yathAshAstraM niShevitAH | 
M6.88c/ yathA.ukta.kAriNaM vipraM nayanti paramAM gatim ||
M6.89a/ sarveShAm api ca-eteShAM veda.smR^itividhAnataH | [M.veda.shrutividhAnataH ]
M6.89c/ gR^ihastha ucyate shreShThaH sa trIn etAn bibharti hi ||
M6.90a/ yathA nadI.nadAH sarve sAgare yAnti saMsthitim |
M6.90c/ tathA-eva-AshramiNaH sarve gR^ihasthe yAnti saMsthitim ||
M6.91a/ caturbhir api ca-eva-etair nityam Ashramibhir dvijaiH |
M6.91c/ dasha.lakShaNako dharmaH sevitavyaH prayatnataH ||
M6.92a/ dhR^itiH kShamA damo 'asteyaM shaucam indriyanigrahaH |
M6.92c/ dhIr vidyA satyam akrodho dashakaM dharmalakShaNam ||
M6.93a/ dasha lakShaNAni dharmasya ye viprAH samadhIyate |
M6.93c/ adhItya ca-anuvartante te yAnti paramAM gatim ||
M6.94a/ dasha.lakShaNakaM dharmam anutiShThan samAhitaH |
M6.94c/ vedAntaM vidhivat-shrutvA saMnyased an.R^iNo dvijaH ||
M6.95a/ saMnyasya sarvakarmANi karmadoShAn apAnudan |
M6.95c/ niyato vedam abhyasya putraishvarye sukhaM vaset ||
M6.96a/ evaM saMnyasya karmANi svakArya.paramo 'a.spR^ihaH |
M6.96c/ saMnyAsena-apahatya-enaH prApnoti paramaM gatim ||
M6.97a/ eSha vo 'abhihito dharmo brAhmaNasya catur.vidhaH |
M6.97c/ puNyo 'akShaya.phalaH pretya rAjJAM dharmaM nibodhata ||

M7.01a/ rAjadharmAn pravakShyAmi yathAvR^itto bhaven nR^ipaH |
M7.01c/ saMbhavash ca yathA tasya siddhish ca paramA yathA ||
M7.02a/ brAhmaM prAptena saMskAraM kShatriyeNa yathAvidhi |
M7.02c/ sarvasya-asya yathAnyAyaM kartavyaM parirakShaNam ||
M7.03a/ a.rAjake hi loke 'asmin sarvato vidruto bhayAt |
M7.03c/ rakShArtham asya sarvasya rAjAnam asR^ijat prabhuH ||
M7.04a/ indra.anila.yama.arkANAm agnesh ca varuNasya ca |
M7.04c/ candra.vitteshayosh ca-eva mAtrA nirhR^itya shAshvatIH ||
M7.05a/ yasmAd eShAM surendrANAM mAtrAbhyo nirmito nR^ipaH |
M7.05c/ tasmAd abhibhavaty eSha sarvabhUtAni tejasA ||
M7.06a/ tapaty Adityavac ca-eSha cakShUMShi ca manAMsi ca |
M7.06c/ na ca-enaM bhuvi shaknoti kash cid apy abhivIkShitum ||
M7.07a/ so 'agnir bhavati vAyush ca so 'arkaH somaH sa dharmarAT |
M7.07c/ sa kuberaH sa varuNaH sa mahendraH prabhAvataH || [M.sa ca-indraH svaprabhAvataH] || [K: ]
M7.08a/ bAlo 'api na-avamAntavyo manuShya iti bhUmipaH |
M7.08c/ mahatI devatA hy eShA nararUpeNa tiShThati ||

M7.19c/ a.samIkShya praNItas tu vinAshayati sarvataH ||

[M7.87Mc/ pAtre pradIyate) yat tu tad dharmasya prasAdhanam // [not in K] 
(Although MedhAtithi comments on the above shloka, Jha's edition does not count it in his numbering of the text. Therefore, Jha ed.'s numbering is the same with K in the following)

M7.87a[88Ma]/ sama.uttama.adhamai rAjA tv AhUtaH pAlayan prajAH |
M7.87c[88Mc]/ na nivarteta saMgrAmAt kShAtraM dharmam anusmaran ||
M7.88a[89Ma]/ saMgrAmeShv anivartitvaM prajAnAM ca-eva pAlanam |
M7.88c[89Mc]/ shushrUShA brAhmaNAnAM ca rAjJAM shreyaskaraM param ||
M7.89a[90Ma]/ AhaveShu mitho 'anyonyaM jighAMsanto mahIkShitaH |
M7.89c[90Mc]/ yudhyamAnAH paraM shaktyA svargaM yAnty a.parAGmukhAH ||

M12.01a/ cAturvarNyasya kR^itsno 'ayam ukto dharmas tvayA-anaghaH |

M12.91c/ samaM pashyann) AtmayAjI svArAjyam adhigacchati) ||
M12.92a/ yathA.uktAny api karmANi parihAya) dvijottamaH |
M12.92c/ AtmajJAne shame ca syAd) vedAbhyAse ca yatnavAn ||
M12.93a/ etadd hi janmasAphalyaM brAhmaNasya visheShataH |
M12.93c/ prApya)-etat kR^ita.kR^ityo hi dvijo bhavati) na-anyathA ||

M12.94a/ pitR^i.deva.manuShyANAM vedash cakShuH sanAtanam |
M12.94c/ ashakyaM ca-aprameyaM ca vedashAstram iti sthitiH ||
M12.95a/ yA vedabAhyAH smR^itayo yAsh ca kAsh ca kudR^iShTayaH | [M.shrutayo ]
M12.95c/ sarvAs tA niSh.phalAH pretya tamo.niShThA hi tAH smR^itAH || 
M12.96a/ utpadyante) cyavante) ca yAny ato 'anyAni kAni cit | [M.utpadyante) vinashyanti) ]
M12.96c/ tAny arvAkkAlikatayA niSh.phalAny anR^itAni ca ||
M12.97a/ cAturvarNyaM trayo lokAsh catvArash ca-AshramAH pR^ithak |
M12.97c/ bhUtaM bhavyaM bhaviShyaM ca sarvaM vedAt prasidhyati) || [M.bhUtaM bhavad bhaviShyaM ca ]
M12.98a/ shabdaH sparshash ca rUpaM ca raso gandhash ca paJcamaH |
M12.98c/ vedAd eva prasUyante) prasUtir guNa.karmataH || 
M12.99a/ bibharti) sarvabhUtAni vedashAstraM sanAtanam |
M12.99c/ tasmAd etat paraM manye) yat-jantor asya sAdhanam ||
M12.100a/ senApatyaM ca rAjyaM ca daNDanetR^itvam eva ca | [M.sainApatyaM ]
M12.100c/ sarvalokAdhipatyaM ca vedashAstravid arhati) ||
M12.101a/ yathA jAta.balo vahnir dahaty) ArdrAn api drumAn |
M12.101c/ tathA dahati) vedajJaH karmajaM doSham AtmanaH ||
M12.102a/ vedashAstrArthatattvajJo yatra tatra-Ashrame vasan) |
M12.102c/ iha-eva loke tiShThan) sa brahmabhUyAya kalpate) ||
M12.103a/ ajJebhyo granthinaH shreShThA granthibhyo dhAriNo varAH |
M12.103c/ dhAribhyo jJAninaH shreShThA jJAnibhyo vyavasAyinaH ||
M12.104a/ tapo vidyA ca viprasya niHshreyasakaraM param |
M12.104c/ tapasA kilbiShaM hanti) vidyayA-amR^itam ashnute) ||
M12.105a/ pratyakShaM ca-anumAnaM ca shAstraM ca vividhA.Agamam |
M12.105c/ trayaM suviditaM kAryaM dharmashuddhim abhIpsatA ||
M12.106a/ ArShaM dharma.upadeshaM ca vedashAstra.avirodhinA |
M12.106c/ yas tarkeNa-anusaMdhatte) sa dharmaM veda) na-itaraH ||
M12.107a/ naiHshreyasam idaM karma yathA.uditam asheShataH |
M12.107c/ mAnavasya-asya shAstrasya rahasyam upadishyate) || [M.upadekShyate ]

M12.108a/ an.AmnAteShu dharmeShu kathaM syAd) iti ced bhavet) |
M12.108c/ yaM shiShTA brAhmaNA brUyuH) sa dharmaH syAd) ashaGkitaH ||
M12.109a/ dharmeNa-adhigato yais tu vedaH sa.paribR^iMhaNaH |
M12.109c/ te shiShTA brAhmaNA jJeyAH shruti.pratyakShahetavaH ||
M12.110a/ dasha.avarA vA pariShadyaM dharmaM parikalpayet) |
M12.110c/ try.avarA vA-api vR^ittasthA taM dharmaM na vicAlayet) ||
M12.111a/ traividyo hetukas tarkI nairukto dharmapAThakaH |
M12.111c/ trayash ca-AshramiNaH pUrve pariShat syAd) dasha.avarA ||
M12.112a/ R^igvedavid yajurvid- ca sAmavedavid eva ca |
M12.112c/ try.avarA pariShad- jJeyA dharmasaMshayanirNaye ||
M12.113a/ eko 'api vedavid dharmaM yaM vyavasyed) dvijottamaH |
M12.113c/ sa vijJeyaH paro dharmo na-ajJAnAm udito 'ayutaiH ||
M12.114a/ a.vratAnAm a.mantrANAM jAtimAtra.upajIvinAm |
M12.114c/ sahasrashaH sametAnAM pariShattvaM na vidyate) ||
M12.115a/ yaM vadanti) tamobhUtA mUrkhA dharmam atadvidaH |
M12.115c/ tatpApaM shatadhA bhUtvA) tadvaktR^iR^in anugacchati) ||
M12.116a/ etad vo 'abhihitaM sarvaM niHshreyasakaraM param |
M12.116c/ asmAd apracyuto vipraH prApnoti) paramAM gatim ||

M12.117a/ evaM sa bhagavAn devo lokAnAM hitakAmyayA |
M12.117c/ dharmasya paramaM guhyaM mama-idaM sarvam uktavAn) ||
M12.118a/ sarvam Atmani saMpashyet) sat-ca-asat-ca samAhitaH |
M12.118c/ sarvaM hy Atmani saMpashyan) na-adharme kurute) manaH || [M.matim ]
M12.119a/ AtmA-eva devatAH sarvAH sarvam Atmany avasthitam |
M12.119c/ AtmA hi janayaty) eShAM karmayogaM sharIriNAm ||
M12.120a/ khaM saMniveshayet) kheShu ceShTana.sparshane 'anilam |
M12.120c/ pakti.dR^iShTyoH paraM tejaH snehe 'apo gAM ca mUrtiShu ||
M12.121a/ manasi-induM dishaH shrotre krAnte viShNuM bale haram |
M12.121c/ vAcy agniM mitram utsarge prajane ca prajApatim ||
M12.122a/ prashAsitAraM sarveShAm aNIyAMsam aNor api |
M12.122c/ rukma.AbhaM svapnadhIgamyaM vidyAt) taM puruShaM param ||
M12.123a/ etam eke vadanty) agniM manum anye prajApatim |
M12.123c/ indram eke pare prANam apare brahma shAshvatam ||
M12.124a/ eSha sarvANi bhUtAni paJcabhir vyApya) mUrtibhiH |
M12.124c/ janma.vR^iddhi.kShayair nityaM saMsArayati) cakravat ||
M12.125a/ evaM yaH sarvabhUteShu pashyaty) AtmAnam AtmanA |
M12.125c/ sa sarvasamatAm etya) brahma-abhyeti) paraM padam |
M12.126a/ ity etan mAnavaM shAstraM bhR^iguproktaM paThan) dvijaH |
M12.126c/ bhavaty) AcAravAn nityaM yathA.iShTAM prApnuyAd) gatim ||
